################
# NAME FORMATS #
################

### REPUBLICS
# Generic Republic 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_military_junta
				has_government = gov_military_commissariat
				has_government = gov_irenic_bureaucracy
				has_government = gov_moral_democracy
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_plutocratic_oligarchy
				has_government = gov_representative_democracy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_timocracy
				has_government = gov_xenophile_democracy
				has_government = gov_republican_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_peoples_republic

# Communist Republic 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 4
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_totalitarian_regime
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_communal_parity
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_soviet_republic
				has_government = gov_bur_collectivism
				has_government = gov_peoples_commissariat
				has_government = gov_communist_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_anarchy_communism
			}
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_materialist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics: Bug Branch
				has_ethic = ethic_cooperative
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_cooperative
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_soviet_republic
				has_government = gov_bur_collectivism
				has_government = gov_peoples_commissariat
				has_government = gov_communist_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_anarchy_communism
				# Empires Expanded
				has_valid_civic = civic_collectivism
			}
			NOR = {
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics: Bug Branch
				has_ethic = ethic_competitive
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_competitive
			}
			OR = {
				has_origin = origin_lost_colony
				has_origin = origin_scion
				has_origin = origin_void_dwellers
				has_origin = origin_separatists
				has_origin = origin_remnants
				# Mod - Distant Origins
				has_origin = origin_mzilli_exiles
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<communist_adj> {AofB{<republic_noun> [This.Capital.System.GetName]}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{<communist_adj> {AofBpfx{[This.Capital.System.GetName] <republic_noun>}}}"

	format = "{<communist_adj> {AofB{<republic_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}}"

	# People's Republic of Earth

# Communist Republic 3
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 4
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_totalitarian_regime
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_communal_parity
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_soviet_republic
				has_government = gov_bur_collectivism
				has_government = gov_peoples_commissariat
				has_government = gov_communist_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_anarchy_communism
			}
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_materialist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics: Bug Branch
				has_ethic = ethic_cooperative
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_cooperative
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_soviet_republic
				has_government = gov_bur_collectivism
				has_government = gov_peoples_commissariat
				has_government = gov_communist_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_anarchy_communism
				# Empires Expanded
				has_valid_civic = civic_collectivism
			}
			NOR = {
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics: Bug Branch
				has_ethic = ethic_competitive
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_competitive
			}
			OR = {
				has_origin = origin_lost_colony
				has_origin = origin_scion
				has_origin = origin_void_dwellers
				has_origin = origin_separatists
				has_origin = origin_remnants
				# Mod - Distant Origins
				has_origin = origin_mzilli_exiles
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{[This.Capital.System.GetAdj] {<communist_adj> {<republic_noun>}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{<communist_adj> {<republic_noun>}}"

### FEDERATIONS
# Generic Federation 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 4
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_military_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_military_junta
				has_government = gov_military_commissariat
				has_government = gov_irenic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_irenic_bureaucracy
				has_government = gov_moral_democracy
				has_government = gov_totalitarian_regime
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_constitutional_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_plutocratic_oligarchy
				has_government = gov_representative_democracy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_timocracy
				has_government = gov_xenophile_democracy
				has_government = gov_republican_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_peoples_republic
				has_government = gov_liberal_democracy
				has_government = gov_social_democracy
				has_government = gov_congress_republic
				has_government = gov_aristocratic_republic
				has_government = gov_oligarchic_republic
				has_government = gov_slaver_republic
				has_government = gov_demos_cratos
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = gov_democratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_strict_democracy
			}
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_lost_colony }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_scion }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_remnants }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_void_dwellers }
			# Mod - Distant Origins
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_mzilli_exiles }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<united_federal_adj> {AofB{<states_pl_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{<united_federal_adj> {AofB{<states_pl_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}}"
	# United Nations of Earth
}

	random_weight = {

		modifier = {
			add = 8
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_military_junta
				has_government = gov_military_commissariat
				has_government = gov_irenic_bureaucracy
				has_government = gov_moral_democracy
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_plutocratic_oligarchy
				has_government = gov_representative_democracy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_xenophile_democracy
				has_government = gov_peoples_republic
				has_government = gov_liberal_democracy
				has_government = gov_social_democracy
				has_government = gov_congress_republic
				has_government = gov_demos_cratos
			}
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
				#Ethics and Civics: Bug Branch
				has_ethic = ethic_competitive
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_competitive
			}
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_lost_colony }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_scion }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_remnants }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_void_dwellers }
			# Mod - Distant Origins
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_mzilli_exiles }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<free_adj> {AofB{<states_pl_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{AofB{<states_pl_noun> <free_adj> {[This.Capital.GetName]}}}"
	# Free Nations of Earth

				has_government = gov_irenic_bureaucracy
				has_government = gov_moral_democracy
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_plutocratic_oligarchy
				has_government = gov_representative_democracy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_xenophile_democracy
				has_government = gov_peoples_republic
				has_government = gov_liberal_democracy
				has_government = gov_social_democracy
				has_government = gov_congress_republic
				has_government = gov_demos_cratos
			}
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			}
			OR = {
				has_origin = origin_lost_colony
				has_origin = origin_scion
				has_origin = origin_void_dwellers
				has_origin = origin_separatists
				num_owned_planets > 1
				# Mod - Distant Origins
				has_origin = origin_mzilli_exiles
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}

	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{AofB{<federation_union_of_noun> <free_adj> {<celestial_bodies_pl_noun>}}}"

				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_soviet_republic
				has_government = gov_bur_collectivism
				has_government = gov_peoples_commissariat
				has_government = gov_communist_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_anarchy_communism
				# Empires Expanded
				has_valid_civic = civic_collectivism
			}
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_lost_colony }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_scion }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_remnants }
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_void_dwellers }
			# Mod - Distant Origins
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_mzilli_exiles }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<communist_adj> {AofB{<federation_union_of_noun> <states_pl_noun>}}}"

### MONARCHIES
# Generic Monarchy 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 4
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_despotic_empire
				has_government = gov_theocratic_monarchy
				has_government = gov_celestial_empire
				has_government = gov_star_empire
				has_government = gov_martial_empire
				has_government = gov_irenic_monarchy
				has_government = gov_despotic_hegemony
				has_government = gov_illuminated_autocracy
				has_government = gov_feudal_empire
				has_government = gov_enlightened_monarchy
				has_government = gov_elective_monarchy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_noble_aristocracy
				has_government = gov_aristocratic_monarchy
				has_government = gov_absolute_monarchy
				has_government = gov_enlighted_socialism
				has_government = gov_par_monarchy
				has_government = gov_genuine_aristocracy
				has_government = gov_great_houses
			}
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_void_dwellers }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_subject = yes }
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }

			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}

	# The Trueborn

			has_government = gov_purity_order
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}

	noun = "{[This.GetSpeciesAdj]}"
	prefix_format = "{<pure_adj> {[This.GetSpeciesName]}}"
	# Human Legion State

### RELIGIONS
# Generic Religion 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 1
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_here_be_dragons }
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_holy_tribunal
				has_government = gov_subversive_cult
				has_government = gov_theocratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_theocratic_oligarchy
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = gov_subversive_cult_fam
			}
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 100
			has_country_flag = radical_cult
		}
	}
	format = "{<the_art_cap> {<religious_order_noun>}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{<religious_order_noun>}"
	# The Order
}

			is_primitive = no

			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }

		modifier = {
			add = 5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 100
			has_country_flag = radical_cult
		}
	}
	format = "{AofB{<religious_order_noun> <the_art> {<awesome_adj> {<oow_gen_noun>}}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{AofB{<religious_order_noun> <the_art> {<awesome_adj> {<oow_gen_noun>}}}}"

				has_government = gov_holy_tribunal

# Bandits and Pirates 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 8
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_bandit_kingdom
				has_government = gov_bandit_commune
				has_government = gov_band_blood
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 100
			AND = {
				is_pirate = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = drone_pirate
					has_country_flag = machine_pirate
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			is_country_type = enclave_mercenary
			has_government = gov_mercenary_enclave
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_materialist }
			any_country = {
				is_species = PREV
				OR = {
					has_government = gov_bandit_kingdom
					has_government = gov_bandit_commune
					has_government = gov_band_blood
					has_government = gov_assembly_of_clans
					has_government = gov_war_council
					has_government = gov_martial_dictatorship
					has_government = gov_martial_empire
				}
			}
		}
	}
	format = "{<bandit_adj> {<bandit_gang_noun>}}"
	noun = "{<bandit_adj> {<bandit_gang_noun>}}"
	# Black Devils
}

# Mercenary Megacorp 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 4
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_megacorporation
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_military_corp
				# Mod - Venture Politics
				has_government = gov_megacooperative
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = gov_megacorporation_fam
				has_government = lrsk_gov_var_gov_private_military_contractor_fam
				# Mod - Government Variety
				has_government = lrsk_gov_var_gov_private_military_contractor
				# Mod - Mercenary Megacorps
				has_valid_civic = civic_uncivil_mercenary_company
				# Ethics and Civics: Bug Branch
				has_government = gov_democratic_megacorporation
				has_government = gov_imperial_megacorporation
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_naval_contractors
				has_valid_civic = civic_private_military_companies
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_military_corp
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = lrsk_gov_var_gov_private_military_contractor_fam
				# Mod - Government Variety
				has_government = lrsk_gov_var_gov_private_military_contractor
				# Mod - Mercenary Megacorps
				has_valid_civic = civic_uncivil_mercenary_company
			}
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 20
			is_country_type = enclave_mercenary
			has_government = gov_mercenary_enclave
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					is_species = PREV
					OR = {
						has_government = gov_bandit_kingdom
						has_government = gov_bandit_commune
						has_government = gov_band_blood
						has_government = gov_assembly_of_clans
						has_government = gov_war_council
						has_government = gov_martial_dictatorship
						has_government = gov_martial_empire
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	format = "{<corp_adj> {<corp_industries_merc>}}"
	noun = "{<corp_adj> {<corp_industries_merc>}}"
	prefix_format = "{<corp_adj> {<corp_industries_merc>}}"

		modifier = {
			add = 4

			}
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}

### MILITARY STATES
# Military State 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 4
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_military_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_military_junta
				has_government = gov_military_commissariat
				has_government = gov_citizen_republic
				has_government = gov_citizen_stratocracy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_jingoism
				has_government = gov_national_socialism
			}
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{AofB{<military_state_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{AofB{<military_state_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}"
	
	# Commissary of Earth
}

			has_government = gov_divine_empire
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			OR = {
				has_origin = origin_lost_colony
				has_origin = origin_scion
				has_origin = origin_void_dwellers
				has_origin = origin_separatists
				has_origin = origin_remnants
				num_owned_planets > 1
				# Mod - Distant Origins
				has_origin = origin_mzilli_exiles
			}
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<divine_adj> {AofB{<imperial_monarchy_noun> [This.Capital.System.GetName]}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "their {<style_holy_noun>}'s"
	# Divine Empire of Sol

			has_government = gov_dimensional_covenant
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 16
			has_government = gov_dimensional_covenant
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
		}
	}
	format = "{AofB{<religious_people_noun> <the_art> {<dimensional_noun>}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{AofB{<religious_people_noun> <the_art> {<dimensional_noun>}}}"

### KNIGHTS OF THE TOXIC GOD

#Stinky Republic 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 50
			has_origin = origin_toxic_knights
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_military_junta
				has_government = gov_military_commissariat
				has_government = gov_irenic_bureaucracy
				has_government = gov_moral_democracy
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_plutocratic_oligarchy
				has_government = gov_representative_democracy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_timocracy
				has_government = gov_xenophile_democracy
				has_government = gov_republican_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_peoples_republic
				has_government = gov_liberal_democracy
				has_government = gov_social_democracy
				has_government = gov_congress_republic
				has_government = gov_aristocratic_republic
				has_government = gov_oligarchic_republic
				has_government = gov_slaver_republic
				has_government = gov_demos_cratos
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = gov_democratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_strict_democracy
			}
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<toxic_adj> {AofB{<republic_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{<toxic_adj> {AofBpfx{<republic_noun> [This.Capital.GetName]}}}"
	#Stinky Republic of Earth
}

				has_government = gov_holy_tribunal
				has_government = gov_subversive_cult
				has_government = gov_theocratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_theocratic_oligarchy
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = gov_subversive_cult_fam
			}
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<the_art_cap> {<necrophage_adj> {<religious_order_noun>}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{<necrophage_adj> {<religious_order_noun>}}"
	# The Hungry Order
}

## FRONTIERS - Currently non-functional due to how F:F's frontier naming works - efforts to jank my way around it
#  were inneffective, but I'll leave these around in case the mod changes or someone else wants to have a go at it.
# Frontier Generic 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 2500	# Just to be safe
			has_origin = origin_frontier_world
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_fanatic_purifiers }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{AofB{<frontier_noun> [This.Capital.System.GetName]}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{AofBpfx{<frontier_noun> [This.Capital.System.GetName]}}"
	# Frontier of Sol
}

# Frontier Megacorp 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10000	# Just to be safe
			has_origin = origin_frontier_world
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_megacorporation
				has_government = gov_trade_league
				has_government = gov_criminal_syndicate
				# Mod - Venture Politics
				has_government = gov_megacooperative
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = gov_megacorporation_fam
				# Civics and Ethics: Bugged Branch
				has_government = gov_democratic_megacorporation
				has_government = gov_imperial_megacorporation
				has_government = gov_democratic_criminal_syndicate
				has_government = gov_imperial_criminal_syndicate
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{[This.Capital.System.GetAdj] {<coporate_frontier_noun>}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{[This.Capital.System.GetAdj] {<coporate_frontier_noun>}}"
	# Solar Subsidiary
}

		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 5
			has_origin = origin_hegira_colony
			OR = {
				has_government = gov_military_junta
				has_government = gov_military_commissariat
				has_government = gov_irenic_bureaucracy
				has_government = gov_moral_democracy
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_direct_democracy
				has_government = gov_plutocratic_oligarchy
				has_government = gov_representative_democracy
				# Mod - Ethics and Civics Classic 3.2
				has_government = gov_timocracy
				has_government = gov_xenophile_democracy
				has_government = gov_republican_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_peoples_republic
				has_government = gov_liberal_democracy
				has_government = gov_social_democracy
				has_government = gov_congress_republic
				has_government = gov_aristocratic_republic
				has_government = gov_oligarchic_republic
				has_government = gov_slaver_republic
				has_government = gov_demos_cratos
				# Mod - More Authorities
				has_government = gov_democratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_strict_democracy
			}
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
		}
	}
	format = "{<hegiran_adj> {[This.Capital.System.GetAdj] {<federation_noun>}}}"
	noun = "{[This.Capital.System.GetName]}"
	prefix_format = "{<hegiran_adj> {[This.Capital.System.GetAdj] {<federation_noun>}}}"
	# Exiled Solar Federation
}
